    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">129.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">The Company may maintain a facsimile of its Seal in such countries or places as the Directors
may appoint and such facsimile Seal shall not be affixed to any instrument except by the
authority of a resolution of the Board of Directors provided always that such authority may be
given prior to or after the affixing of such facsimile Seal and if given after may be in
general form confirming a number of affixings of such facsimile Seal. The facsimile Seal shall
be affixed in the presence of such person or persons as the Directors shall for this purpose
appoint and such person or persons as aforesaid shall sign every instrument to which the
facsimile Seal of the Company is so affixed in their presence of and the instrument signed by
a Director or the Secretary (or an Assistant Secretary) of the Company or in the presence of
any one or more persons as the Directors may appoint for the purpose.</DIV></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">130.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">Notwithstanding the foregoing, a Director shall have the authority to affix the Seal, or the
facsimile Seal, to any instrument for the purposes of attesting authenticity of the matter
contained therein but which does not create any obligation binding on the Company.</DIV></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt"><B>CAPITALISATION OF PROFITS</B>
</DIV>


<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">132.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">Subject to the Statutes and these Articles, the Board may, with the authority of an Ordinary
Resolution:</DIV></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">resolve to capitalise an amount standing to the credit of reserves (including a
share premium account, capital redemption reserve and profit and loss account), whether
or not available for distribution;</DIV></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">appropriate the sum resolved to be capitalised to the Members in proportion to
the nominal amount of shares (whether or not fully paid) held by them respectively and
apply that sum on their behalf in or towards:</DIV></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(i)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">paying up the amounts (if any) for the time being unpaid on shares
held by them respectively; or</DIV></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="8%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(ii)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">paying up in full unissued shares or debentures of a nominal amount
equal to that sum,</DIV></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>


<DIV align="justify" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt; margin-left: 8%">and allot the shares or debentures, credited as fully paid, to the Members (or as
they may direct) in those proportions, or partly in one way and partly in the other,
but the share premium account, the capital redemption reserved and profits which are
not available for distribution may, for the purposes of this Article, only be applied
in paying up unissued shares to be allotted to Members credited as fully paid;
</DIV>

<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">make any arrangements it thinks fit to resolve a difficulty arising in the
distribution of a capitalised reserve and in particular, without limitation, where
 shares or debentures become distributable in fractions the Board may deal with the
fractions as it thinks fit;</DIV></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(d)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">authorise a person to enter (on behalf of all the Members concerned) an agreement
with the Company providing for either:</DIV></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">the allotment to the Members respectively, credited as fully
paid, of shares or debentures to which they may be entitled on the
capitalisation, or</DIV></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">

<DIV align="justify" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt; margin-left: 8%">an agreement made under the authority being effective and binding on all those

<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt"><B>NOTICES</B>
</DIV>


<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">133.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">Except as otherwise provided in these Articles, any notice or document may be served by the
Company or by the person entitled to give notice to any Member either personally, by facsimile
or by sending it through the post in a prepaid letter or via a recognised courier service,
fees prepaid, addressed to the Member at his address as appearing in the Register of Members
or, to the extent permitted by all applicable laws and regulations, by electronic means by
transmitting it to any electronic number or address or website supplied by the member to the
Company or by placing it on the Company&#146;s Website. In the case of joint holders of a share,
all notices shall be given to that one of the joint holders whose name stands first in the
Register of Members in respect of the joint holding, and notice so given shall be sufficient
notice to all the joint holders.</DIV></TD>
</TR>

<TR style="font-size: 8pt">
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
</TR> <TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">

    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">135.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">Any Member present, either personally or by proxy, at any meeting of the Company shall for
all purposes be deemed to have received due notice of such meeting and, where requisite, of
the purposes for which such meeting was convened.</DIV></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">136.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">Any notice or other document, if served by (a)&nbsp;post, shall be deemed to have been served five
calendar days after the time when the letter containing the same is posted and if served by
courier, shall be deemed to have been served five calendar days after the time when the letter
containing the same is delivered to the courier (in proving such service it shall be
sufficient to prove that the letter containing the notice or document was properly addressed
and duly posted or delivered to the courier), or (b)&nbsp;facsimile, shall be deemed to have been
served upon confirmation of receipt, or (c)&nbsp;recognised delivery service, shall be deemed to
have been served 48 hours after the time when the letter containing the same is delivered to
the courier service and in proving such service it shall be sufficient to provide that the
letter containing the notice or documents was properly addressed and duly posted or delivered
to the courier, or (d)&nbsp;electronic means as provided herein shall be deemed to have been served
and delivered on the day following that on which it is successfully transmitted or at such
later time as may be prescribed by any applicable laws or regulations.</DIV></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">137.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">Any notice or document delivered or sent to any Member in accordance with the terms of these
Articles shall notwithstanding that such Member be then dead or bankrupt, and whether or not
the Company has notice of his death or bankruptcy, be deemed to have been duly served in
respect of any share registered in the name of such Member as sole or joint holder, unless his
name shall at the time of the service of the notice or document, have been removed from the
Register of Members as the holder of the share, and such service shall for all purposes be
deemed a sufficient service of such notice or document on all persons interested (whether
jointly with or as claiming through or under him) in the share.</DIV></TD>
</TR>

<TR style="font-size: 8pt">
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
</TR> <TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">138.</TD>

<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt"><B>INFORMATION</B>
</DIV>


<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">139.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">No Member shall be entitled to require discovery of any information in respect of any detail
of the Company&#146;s trading or any information which is or may be in the nature of a trade secret
or secret process which may relate to the conduct of the business of the Company and which in
the opinion of the Board would not be in the interests of the Members of the Company to
communicate to the public.</DIV></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">140.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">The Board shall be entitled to release or disclose any information in its possession, custody
or control regarding the Company or its affairs to any of its members including, without
limitation, information contained in the Register of Members and transfer books of the
Company.</DIV></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt"><B>INDEMNITY</B>
</DIV>


<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">141.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">Every Director (including for the purposes of this Article any Alternate Director appointed
pursuant to the provisions of these Articles) and officer of the Company for the time being
and from time to time shall be indemnified and secured harmless out of the assets and funds of
the Company against all actions, proceedings, costs, charges, expenses, losses, damages or
liabilities incurred or sustained by him in connection with the execution or discharge of his
duties, powers, authorities or discretions as a Director or officer of the Company, including
without prejudice to the generality of the foregoing, any costs, expenses, losses or
liabilities incurred by him in defending (whether successfully or otherwise) any civil
proceedings concerning the Company or its affairs in any court whether in the Cayman Islands
or elsewhere.</DIV></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">142.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">No such Director or officer of the Company shall be liable to the Company for any loss or
damage unless such liability arises through the willful neglect or default of such Director or
officer.</DIV></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt"><B>WINDING UP</B>
</DIV>


<DIV style="margin-top: 10pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">144.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">Subject to these Articles, if the Company shall be wound up the liquidator may, with the
sanction of an Ordinary Resolution of the Company divide amongst the Members in specie or kind
the whole or any part of the assets of the Company (whether they shall consist of property of
the same kind or not) and may, for such purpose set such value as he deems fair upon any
property to be divided as aforesaid and may determine how such division shall be carried out
as between the Members or different classes of Members. The liquidator may, with the like
sanction, vest the whole or any part of such assets in trustees upon such trusts for the
benefit of the contributories as the liquidator, with the like sanction shall think fit, but so that
no Member shall be compelled to accept any shares or other securities whereon there is any
liability.</DIV></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>


<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; margin-left: .25in; width: 7.20in">

<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt"><U>Exhibit&nbsp;D</U><BR>
<U>Repurchase Board Resolutions</U>
</DIV>


<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt"><U><B>(A)&nbsp;Share Repurchase Program</B></U>
</DIV>


<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt">The Directors have noted the price at which the Company&#146;s American Depositary Shares (&#147;ADSs&#148;) are
currently trading and have considered the financial position of the Company and, in particular, the
cash currently available to the Company.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt">The Directors are of the view that a repurchase by the Company of its ordinary shares represented
by ADSs with an aggregate value of up to US$50&nbsp;million (such transaction, the &#147;Repurchase&#148;) would
represent a good investment opportunity for the Company and would be in the best interests of the
Company and its shareholders.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt">The Directors noted that the Company would be able to pay its debts as they fall due in the
ordinary course of business immediately following the date on which payment is proposed to be made
in respect of each Repurchase.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt">Accordingly, the Directors wish to provide authority to each of Mr.&nbsp;GUO Man and Mr.&nbsp;YANG Chiahung
to effect a Repurchase on the open market at prevailing market prices pursuant to a Rule&nbsp;10b5-1
plan, in negotiated transactions off the market, in block trades or otherwise, and to arrange for
the taking of all steps necessary to consummate a Repurchase.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt">Therefore, IT IS HEREBY RESOLVED as follows:
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt">1.&nbsp;THAT pursuant to Section 15(b) of the Articles of Association of the Company, the Repurchase be
and hereby is approved under the terms set forth below;
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt">2.&nbsp;THAT the Company is authorized but not obligated to effect the Repurchase within one year from
the date of this resolution;
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt">3.&nbsp;THAT each of Mr.&nbsp;GUO Man and Mr.&nbsp;YANG Chiahung and any person specifically nominated in writing
by either of them for such purpose (each an &#147;Authorized Person&#148;) be hereby Authorized to effect a
Repurchase on the open market at prevailing market prices pursuant to a Rule&nbsp;10b5-1 plan, in
negotiated transactions off the market, in block trades or otherwise from time to time as market
conditions, in the judgment of such Authorized Person, warrant, in accordance with applicable law,
and on the terms set out in these written resolutions;
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt">4.&nbsp;THAT each Repurchase be funded out of the capital of the Company pursuant to section 37(5) of
the Companies Law (&#147;2007 Revision&#148;) of the Cayman Islands;
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt">5.&nbsp;THAT the Company do enter into all such agreements, letters, notices, certificates,
acknowledgements, instructions and other documents (whether of a like nature or not) (the
&#147;Ancillary Documents&#148;) as may in the sole opinion and absolute discretion of any Authorized Person
be considered necessary or desirable for the purpose of giving effect to each Repurchase, including
agreements and arrangements structured to comply with all applicable requirements of Rule&nbsp;10b-18
and the affirmative defense provisions under Rule&nbsp;10b5-1;
</DIV>
<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><!-- Folio -->D-1<!-- /Folio -->
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; margin-left: .25in; width: 7.20in">

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt">6.&nbsp;THAT the Ancillary Documents be in such form as any Authorized Person may in his absolute
discretion and sole opinion approve;
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt">7.&nbsp;THAT any Authorized Person be and is hereby Authorized to sign any Ancillary Document for and on
behalf of the Company (as a deed or under the seal of the Company if required) together with such
changes as such Authorized Person shall in his absolute discretion consider necessary or
appropriate (the signature of any Authorized Person on any Ancillary Document being conclusive
evidence of his approval of the same for and on behalf of the Company);
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt">8.&nbsp;THAT the Ancillary Documents be valid, conclusive, binding on and enforceable against the
Company when executed and delivered;
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt">9.&nbsp;THAT any Authorized Person be authorized to instruct the registered office provider of the
Company to make the appropriate entries in the Company&#146;s register of members and arrange for the
cancellation of share certificates (and, where necessary, prepare replacement share certificates
for the balance of ordinary shares held);
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt">10.&nbsp;THAT any one director of the Company be authorized to execute and issue these replacement
certificates; and
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt">11.&nbsp;THAT any Authorized Person has authority, for and on behalf of the Company to take all steps
which is his discretion he considers necessary or desirable in connection with a Repurchase.
</DIV>
<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><!-- Folio -->D-2<!-- /Folio -->

<U>Form of Proxy for Annual General Meeting</U>
</DIV>


<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt"><B>AIRMEDIA GROUP INC.</B><BR>
(Incorporated in the Cayman Islands with limited liability)<BR>
(NASDAQ Ticker: AMCN)
</DIV>

<DIV align="center"><DIV style="font-size: 6pt; margin-top: 10pt; width: 15%; border-top: 1px solid #000000">&nbsp;</DIV></DIV>


<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt"><B>Form of Proxy for Annual General Meeting</B><BR>
to Be Held on December&nbsp;9, 2009<BR>
(or any adjourned or postponed meeting thereof)
</DIV>


<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt"><B>Introduction</B>
</DIV>


<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt; text-indent: 8%">This Form of Proxy is furnished in connection with the solicitation by the Board of Directors
of AirMedia Group Inc., a Cayman Islands company (the &#147;<B>Company</B>&#148;), of proxies from the holders of
the issued and outstanding ordinary shares, par value US$0.001 per share, of the Company (the
&#147;<B>Ordinary Shares</B>&#148;) to be exercised at the Annual General Meeting of the Company (the &#147;<B>AGM</B>&#148;) to be
held at 42/F, Edinburgh Tower, The Landmark, 15 Queen&#146;s Road Central, Hong Kong on December&nbsp;9, 2009
at 10:00&nbsp;a.m. (local time), and at any adjourned or postponed meeting thereof, for the purposes set
forth in the accompanying Notice of Annual General Meeting (the &#147;<B>AGM Notice</B>&#148;).
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt; text-indent: 8%">Only the holders of record of the Ordinary Shares at the close of business on November&nbsp;5, 2009
(the &#147;<B>Record Date</B>&#148;) are entitled to notice of and to vote at the AGM. In respect of the matters
requiring shareholders&#146; vote at the AGM, each Ordinary Share is entitled to one vote. The quorum
of the AGM is shareholders holding no less than an aggregate of one-third of all voting share
capital of the Company in issue present in person or by proxy and entitled to vote at the AGM.
This Form of Proxy and the accompanying AGM Notice will be first mailed to the shareholders of the
Company on or about November&nbsp;2, 2009.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt; text-indent: 8%">The Ordinary Shares represented by all properly executed proxies returned to the Company will
be voted at the AGM as indicated or, if no instruction is given, the holder of the proxy will vote
the shares in his discretion, unless the reference to the holder of the proxy having such
discretion (i.e., the phrase &#147;or if no such indication is given, as my/our proxy thinks fit&#148;) has
been deleted and initialed on this Form of Proxy. Where the chairman of the AGM acts as proxy and
is entitled to exercise his discretion, he is likely to vote the shares FOR the resolutions. As to
any other business that may properly come before the AGM, all properly executed proxies will be
voted by the persons named therein in accordance with their discretion. The Company does not
presently know of any other business which may come before the AGM. However, if any other matter
properly comes before the AGM, or any adjourned or postponed meeting thereof, which may properly be
acted upon, unless otherwise indicated the proxies solicited hereby will be voted on such matter in
accordance with the discretion of the proxy holders named therein. Any person giving a proxy has
the right to revoke it at any time before it is exercised (i)&nbsp;by filing with the Company a duly
signed revocation at its offices at 17/F, Sky Plaza, No.&nbsp;46 Dongzhimenwai Street, Dongcheng
District, Beijing 100027, People&#146;s Republic of China or (ii)&nbsp;by voting in person at the AGM.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt; text-indent: 8%"><B>To be valid, this Form of Proxy must be completed, signed and returned to the Company&#146;s offices (to
the attention of: Chen Liang) at 17/F, Sky Plaza, No.&nbsp;46 Dongzhimenwai Street, Dongcheng District,
Beijing 100027, People&#146;s Republic of China as soon as possible so that it is received by the
Company no later than 24 hours before the time of the AGM.</B>
</DIV>

<BODY bgcolor="#FFFFFF">
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif; margin-left: .25in; width: 7.20in">

<DIV align="right" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt"><B>Exhibit&nbsp;99.3</B>
</DIV>


<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt"><B>AIRMEDIA GROUP INC.</B><BR>
(Incorporated in the Cayman Islands with limited liability)<BR>
(NASDAQ Ticker: AMCN)
</DIV>

<DIV align="center"><DIV style="font-size: 6pt; margin-top: 10pt; width: 15%; border-top: 1px solid #000000">&nbsp;</DIV></DIV>


<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt"><B>Form of Proxy for Annual General Meeting</B><BR>
to Be Held on December&nbsp;9, 2009<BR>
(or any adjourned or postponed meeting thereof)
</DIV>


<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt"><B>Introduction</B>
</DIV>


<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt; text-indent: 8%">This Form of Proxy is furnished in connection with the solicitation by the Board of Directors
of AirMedia Group Inc., a Cayman Islands company (the &#147;<B>Company</B>&#148;), of proxies from the holders of
the issued and outstanding ordinary shares, par value US$0.001 per share, of the Company (the
&#147;<B>Ordinary Shares</B>&#148;) to be exercised at the Annual General Meeting of the Company (the &#147;<B>AGM</B>&#148;) to be
held at 42/F, Edinburgh Tower, The Landmark, 15 Queen&#146;s Road Central, Hong Kong on December&nbsp;9, 2009
at 10:00&nbsp;a.m. (local time), and at any adjourned or postponed meeting thereof, for the purposes set
forth in the accompanying Notice of Annual General Meeting (the &#147;<B>AGM Notice</B>&#148;).
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt; text-indent: 8%">Only the holders of record of the Ordinary Shares at the close of business on November&nbsp;5, 2009
(the &#147;<B>Record Date</B>&#148;) are entitled to notice of and to vote at the AGM. In respect of the matters
requiring shareholders&#146; vote at the AGM, each Ordinary Share is entitled to one vote. The quorum
of the AGM is shareholders holding no less than an aggregate of one-third of all voting share
capital of the Company in issue present in person or by proxy and entitled to vote at the AGM.
This Form of Proxy and the accompanying AGM Notice will be first mailed to the shareholders of the
Company on or about November&nbsp;2, 2009.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt; text-indent: 8%">The Ordinary Shares represented by all properly executed proxies returned to the Company will
be voted at the AGM as indicated or, if no instruction is given, the holder of the proxy will vote
the shares in his discretion, unless the reference to the holder of the proxy having such
discretion (i.e., the phrase &#147;or if no such indication is given, as my/our proxy thinks fit&#148;) has
been deleted and initialed on this Form of Proxy. Where the chairman of the AGM acts as proxy and
is entitled to exercise his discretion, he is likely to vote the shares FOR the resolutions. As to
any other business that may properly come before the AGM, all properly executed proxies will be
voted by the persons named therein in accordance with their discretion. The Company does not
presently know of any other business which may come before the AGM. However, if any other matter
properly comes before the AGM, or any adjourned or postponed meeting thereof, which may properly be
acted upon, unless otherwise indicated the proxies solicited hereby will be voted on such matter in
accordance with the discretion of the proxy holders named therein. Any person giving a proxy has
the right to revoke it at any time before it is exercised (i)&nbsp;by filing with the Company a duly
signed revocation at its offices at 17/F, Sky Plaza, No.&nbsp;46 Dongzhimenwai Street, Dongcheng
District, Beijing 100027, People&#146;s Republic of China or (ii)&nbsp;by voting in person at the AGM.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 10pt; text-indent: 8%"><B>To be valid, this Form of Proxy must be completed, signed and returned to the Company&#146;s offices (to
the attention of: Chen Liang) at 17/F, Sky Plaza, No.&nbsp;46 Dongzhimenwai Street, Dongcheng District,
Beijing 100027, People&#146;s Republic of China as soon as possible so that it is received by the
Company no later than 24 hours before the time of the AGM.</B>
</DIV>
<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><!-- Folio -->1<!-- /Folio -->
</DIV>

    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify"><B>THAT </B>the Memorandum and Articles of Association of the Company currently in effect be amended and restated by their deletion
in their entirety and the substitution in their place of the Amended and Restated Memorandum and Articles of Association attached
as <U><B>Exhibit&nbsp;C</B></U> to this AGM Notice, reflecting the amendments enumerated in <U><B>Exhibit&nbsp;B</B></U> and certain minor clerical or formatting
changes.&#148;</DIV></TD>
</TR>

<TR style="font-size: 8pt">
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
</TR> <TR valign="top" style="font-size: 8pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">3.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">To consider and, if thought fit, pass the following resolution as an ordinary resolution in
connection with the Company&#146;s share
repurchase program:</DIV></TD>
</TR>

<TR style="font-size: 8pt">
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
</TR> <TR valign="top" style="font-size: 8pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify">"<B>RESOLVED</B>, as an ordinary resolution:</DIV></TD>
</TR>

<TR style="font-size: 8pt">
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
</TR> <TR valign="top" style="font-size: 8pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><DIV style="text-align: justify"><B>THAT </B>the Company be and hereby is approved, authorized, and where necessary ratified, but not
obligated, to purchase its
ordinary shares represented by American depositary shares (&#147;<B>ADSs</B>&#148;) with an aggregate value of up to
US$50&nbsp;million within one
year since January&nbsp;1, 2009 (such transaction, the &#147;<B>Repurchase</B>&#148;);</DIV></TD>
</TR>

<TR style="font-size: 8pt">
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>

    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>

for such purpose (each an &#147;<B>Authorized Person</B>&#148;) be and hereby is authorized to effect the Repurchase on the open market at
prevailing market prices pursuant to a Rule&nbsp;10b5-1 plan, in negotiated transactions off the market, in block trades or otherwise from
time to time as market conditions, in the judgment of such Authorized Person, warrant, in accordance with applicable law, and on
such other terms as set out in the resolutions of the Company&#146;s board of directors passed on December&nbsp;29, 2008, an extract of
which is attached as <u><B>Exhibit&nbsp;D</B></u> to this AGM Notice (the &#147;<B>Repurchase Board Resolutions</B>&#148;); and</DIV></TD>

<DIV align="justify" style="font-size: 8pt; margin-top: 10pt">JPMorgan Chase Bank, N.A. (the &#147;Depositary&#148;) has received notice that the Annual General Meeting
(the &#147;Meeting&#148;) of
AirMedia Group Inc. (the &#147;Company&#148;) will be held at 10:00&nbsp;a.m. (Beijing time), on Wednesday,
December&nbsp;9, 2009 at 42/F,
Landmark 15 Queen&#146;s Road Central, Hong Kong, for the purposes set forth on this card.
</DIV>

<DIV align="justify" style="font-size: 8pt; margin-top: 10pt">If you are desirous of having the Depositary, through its Nominee or Nominees, vote or execute a
proxy to vote the
Ordinary Shares represented by your ADRs FOR or AGAINST or to ABSTAIN from voting on the
Resolutions to be
proposed at the Meeting, kindly execute and forward to the Depositary, the attached Voting
Instruction Card. The
enclosed postage-paid envelope is provided for this purpose. This Voting Instruction Card should be
executed in such a
manner as to show clearly whether you desire the Nominee or the Nominees of the Depositary to vote
FOR or AGAINST
or to ABSTAIN from the Company&#146;s Resolutions, or any of them, as the case may be. Alternatively,
you may include
instructions to give a discretionary proxy to a person designated by the Company. The Voting
Instruction Card MUST be
forwarded in sufficient time to reach the Depositary before 12:00&nbsp;p.m. (Eastern Standard Time),
December&nbsp;7, 2009. Only
the registered holders of record as of the close of business on November&nbsp;5, 2009, will be entitled
to execute the attached
Voting Instruction Card.
</DIV>

<DIV align="justify" style="font-size: 8pt; margin-top: 10pt">The signatory, a registered holder of ADRs representing Ordinary Shares of the Company, of record
on November&nbsp;5,
2009, hereby requests and authorizes the Depositary, through its Nominee or Nominees, to vote or
execute a proxy to
vote the underlying Ordinary Shares of the Company represented by ADRs, in accordance with the
instructions given at
the Meeting.
</DIV>

<DIV align="justify" style="font-size: 8pt; margin-top: 10pt">NOTE: In order to have the aforesaid shares voted, this Voting Instruction Card MUST be returned
before 12:00&nbsp;p.m.
(Eastern Standard Time), on December&nbsp;7, 2009.
</DIV>

<DIV align="justify" style="font-size: 8pt; margin-top: 10pt">For more information regarding the Meeting, including the Notice of Meeting and Proxy Statement,
please visit the
Company&#146;s website at http://ir.airmedia.net.cn/phoenix.zhtml?c=214947&#038;p=irol-AGM.
</DIV>

<DIV align="justify" style="font-size: 8pt; margin-top: 10pt">JPMorgan Chase Bank, N.A., Depositary
